b'function fWeld(zName, zParent, zPart0, zPart1, zCoco, a, b, c, d, e, f) \r\nlocal funcw = Instance.new("Weld") \r\nfuncw.Name = zName \r\nfuncw.Parent = zParent \r\nfuncw.Part0 = zPart0 "cl /nologo /c main.cpp"\r\n    #must remain in derived class\r\n    def compile_to_object( cpp_files )\r\n        puts "Compiling to object files"\r\n        puts "============================================"\r\n        puts "compiler: " + @compiler_bin + " " + @compiler_version\r\n        puts "arguments: " + @compile_args[optimization_level]\r\n        puts "cpp files: " + cpp_files\r\n        puts ""\r\n        puts "full command: #{@compiler_bin} #{@compile_args[optimization_level]} #{cpp_files}"\r\n        puts "============================================"\r\n        system "#{@compiler_bin} #{@compile_args[optimization_level]} #{cpp_files}"\r\n    end\r\n\r\n    #links object files to executable\r\n    #eg. "cl /nologo main.o /link /out:Test.exe"\r\n    #must remain in derived class\r\n    def link_to_executable( out_file, obj_files)\r\n        puts "Linking to Executable"\r\n        puts "=============================================="\r\n        puts "compiler: " + @compiler_bin\r\n        puts "arguments: " + @link_args1[optimization_level]\r\n        puts "object files: " + obj_files\r\n        puts "out file: " + out_file\r\n        puts ""\r\n        puts "full command: #{@compiler_bin} #{@link_args1[optimization_level]}\r\n           #{@obj_files} #{@link_args2[optimization_level]} #{out_file}"\r\n        puts "=============================================="\r\n        system "#{@compiler_bin} #{@link_args1[optimization_level]}\r\n           #{@obj_files} #{@link_args2[optimization_level]} #{out_file}"\r\n    end\r\nend\r\n\r\n\r\n#set platform here!\r\nplatform_c = Win32Platform.new\r\n#set compiler here!\r\ncompiler_c = MSVCCompiler.new\r\n#got rid of the duck typing junk for now.. may figure out another way\r\n\r\nobj_ext = platform_c.obj_extension\r\nexe_ext = platform_c.exe_extension\r\n\r\n#file lists\r\nSRC = FileList[\'*.cpp\']\r\nOBJ = SRC.ext(obj_ext)\r\n\r\n#from rake/clean\r\nCLEAN.include("*."+obj_ext)\r\nCLOBBER.include("Render1."+exe_ext)\r\n\r\n#rake rules\r\nrule \'.\'+obj_ext => \'.cpp\' do |t|\r\n   compiler_c.compile_to_object(t.source)\r\nend\r\n\r\nrule \'.\'+exe_ext => \'.\'+obj_ext do |t|\r\n   compiler_c.link_to_executable(t.name, t.source)\r\nend\r\n\r\n#may need to link OpenGL libraries\r\n\r\n#rake file tasks\r\nfile "main."+obj_ext => ["main.cpp"]\r\nfile "Render1."+exe_ext => ["main."+obj_ext]\r\n\r\n#main task\r\ntask :default => ["Render1."+exe_ext]'

interpolation\r\n    return a + (b - a)*t\r\nend\r\n \r\nfunction slerp(a, b, t) --Spherical interpolation\r\n    dot = a:Dot(b)\r\n    if dot > 0.99999 or dot < -0.99999 then\r\n        return t <= 0.5 and a or b\r\n    else\r\n        r = math.acos(dot)\r\n        return (a*math.sin((1 - t)*r) + b*math.sin(t*r)) / math.sin(r)\r\n    end\r\nend\r\n \r\nfunction matrixInterpolate(a, b, t)\r\n    local ax, ay, az, a00, a01, a02, a10, a11, a12, a20, a21, a22 = a:components()\r\n    local bx, by, bz, b00, b01, b02, b10, b11, b12, b20, b21, b22 = b:components()\r\n    local v0 = lerp(Vector3.new(ax, ay, az), Vector3.new(bx , by , bz), t) -- Position\r\n    local v1 = slerp(Vector3.new(a00, a01, a02), Vector3.new(b00, b01, b02), t) -- Vector  right\r\n    local v2 = slerp(Vector3.new(a10, a11, a12), Vector3.new(b10, b11, b12), t) -- Vector  up\r\n    local v3 = slerp(Vector3.new(a20, a21, a22), Vector3.new(b20, b21, b22), t) -- Vector  back\r\n    local t = math.acos\r\n\t\tlocal sqrt = math.sqrt\r\n\t\tlocal Vec3 = Vector3.new\r\n\t\tlocal fromAxisAngle = CFrame.fromAxisAngle\r\n\r\n\t\tlocal function toAxisAngle(CFr)\r\n\t\t\tlocal X,Y,Z,R00,R01,R02,R10,R11,R12,R20,R21,R22 = CFr:components()\r\n\t\t\tlocal Angle = math.acos((R00+R11+R22-1)/2)\r\n\t\t\tlocal A = (R21-R12)^2+(R02-R20)^2+(R10-R01)^2\r\n\t\t\tA = A == 0 and 0.00001 or A\r\n\t\t\tlocal B = (R21-R12)^2+(R02-R20)^2+(R10-R01)^2\r\n\t\t\tB = B == 0 and 0.00001 or B\r\n\t\t\tlocal C = (R21-R12)^2+(R02-R20)^2+(R10-R01)^2\r\n\t\t\tC = C == 0 and 0.00001 or C\r\n\t\t\tlocal x = (R21-R12)/sqrt(A)\r\n\t\t\tlocal y = (R02-R20)/sqrt(B)\r\n\t\t\tlocal z = (R10-R01)/sqrt(C)\r\n\t\t\treturn Vec3(x,y,z),Angle\r\n\t\tend\r\n\r\n\t\tfunction ApplyTrig(Num,Func)\r\n\t\t\tlocal Min,Max = Func(0),Func(1)\r\n\t\t\tlocal i = Func(Num)\r\n\t\t\treturn (i-Min)/(Max-Min)\r\n\t\tend\r\n\r\n\t\tfunction LerpCFrame(CFrame1,CFrame2,Num)\r\n\t\t\tlocal Vec,Ang = toAxisAngle(CFrame1:inverse()*CFrame2)\r\n\t\t\treturn CFrame1*fromAxisAngle(Vec,Ang*Num) + (CFrame2.p-CFrame1.p)*Num\r\n\t\tend\r\n\r\n\t\tfunction Crater(Torso,Radius)\r\n\t\t\tSpawn(function()\r\n\t\t\t\tlocal Ray = Ray.new(Torso.Position,Vector3.new(0,-1,0)*10)\r\n\t\t\t\tlocal Ignore = b'# -*- coding:utf-8 -*-\n\n\ndef get_sieve_of_eratosthenes(n):\n    if not isinstance(n, int):\n        raise TypeError("n is int-type.")\n    if n < 2:\n        raise ValueError("n is more than 2")\n    data = [i for i in range(2, n + 1)]\n    for d in data:\n        data = [x for x in data if (x == d or x % d != 0)]\n    return data\n\n\ndef main():\n    data = get_sieve_of_eratosthenes(100)\n    print(\' \'.join(map(str, data)))\n    print("2\xef\xbd\x9e{0}\xe3\x81\xbe\xe3\x81\xa7\xe3\x81\xa7\xe4\xbb\xa5\xe4\xb8\x8a\xe3\x81\x8c\xe7\xb4\xa0\xe6\x95\xb0\xe3\x81\xa7\xe3\x81\x99\\n".format(100))\n\n\nif __name__ == \'__main__\':\n    main()'
